msg:1. The flushing force of the toilet in the room is not good. I flushed it several times on the first day of use.
2. There is no luggage rack. The suitcase is placed on the ground, which is very inconvenient to use.
3. I called the landline one-touch "reception". A male waiter answered the phone. I said I wanted a children's bathrobe. He said he would ask for me, and there was no follow-up. I went out for dinner and asked the front desk again. The front desk said that they didn't know who answered the call and told me to send it to me. Later, they told me that there was no children's bathrobe. The next day, I needed to call and hung up in a hurry!
4. When I checked in, I said I might stay longer. The front desk said to keep it for me first. I asked if it was still the same price. The front desk said that Ctrip could book it. The next morning, Ctrip was full of this room type. In the afternoon, the hotel called to ask if I would stay longer. A lady service staff had a cold and arrogant tone. I told her that the website was full. She asked me to book a big bed. I said the original room? She said that she didn't need to change the room. I explained the situation yesterday. She said to check it out. It seems that she didn't see the relevant information when she asked by phone. My request to stay longer at the original price was expressed tactfully, and the service staff refused firmly. The process standard was indeed in place.
5. When I extended my stay, there was only one service staff at the front desk, and her attitude was gentle, but she could not charge the first-day price. There was no other way. The system and policy were like this, so I didn't blame her. In the middle of my processing, the only front desk receptionist received a long phone call, and two guests came to cut in line to deposit their belongings. She was very busy, and I also felt that she tried to ask the guests to wait for me to continue processing, but there was no suitable way to solve it, so I waited for a long time. When I was able to continue processing, I said that the toilet was not working well. Can I change the room? She said that the hotel was full and the only room that could be changed was worse than my room. At that time, the website had opened a lot of room types available. I understand that I can't upgrade and can't charge the first-day price, but the expression is a bit anxious. But for a hotel of this size, one receptionist is a bit too few, even at night.
6. Although I don't know how the breakfast and upgraded rooms mentioned in the online reviews were achieved, I can understand the difference in service between staying in room 600 and room 1300.
7. Finally, I would like to praise the room service staff for being very friendly. They would say hello when they met us, they looked in good spirits, and they were very polite when delivering gifts. Of course, this is normal etiquette for a hotel of this level, but it was still very kind of them to do so.
